Hello, friends!

This page tracks pets that are in pound_release. The page has grown too long for one petpage, and as a result, it contains only the FAQ, updates, and pets with names starting with A-K. For L-T pets, RW pets, RN pets, 3L/4L pets, links, and credits, please visit /~Fossilise. If you find a new pet or a pet that has already been released/adopted, please send me a Neomail. Contributions are always welcome!

If you would like to see pound_release up and running again (which I'm sure you would or you wouldn't be here), there's a new petition asking for it to reopen! You can read/sign it at /~Xach.

  • January 17, 2020 Big news here! The page has moved from /~Krazy_Karma to /~Poundal, which you probably already figured out or you wouldn't be here. There were nearly 4900 new pets that needed to be added since our last update in the fall, mainly from all the stuck searching that people were doing in November. While I appreciate everyone's additions, it was an awful and horrible and exhausting process and I never want to go this long between updates again.

    I've added a section for 3L/4L names, but removed the sections that listed pets by species and pets by color. If you used those sections in the past, please send me a NM and I'll see if there are enough responses to add them back.

    • Frequently Asked Questions

    Let's answer some of those questions!

    Please consult this list before Neomailing me your questions! If you do not see your question answered, feel free to Neomail me!

  • Are pets being currently released from pound_release?
    • No.

  • Will pets be released from pound_release in the future?
    • We don't know. gutterfoot, one of the TNT developers, responded to a question in the December 18, 2020 Neopian Times editorial with the following:
    Although the flash deadline is over, we're still far from completing our general flash goals. There's a lot of work that still needs to be done, but luckily the updated Pound is something that's coming soon. As we work on converting that, I'll have the team take another look at pound_release.


  • Okay, now that we've gotten that out of the way … what is pound_release (PR)?
    • pound_release is a frozen account created by TNT. When the pound went down for maintenance from 2007-2008, TNT created these frozen accounts to hold the pets rather than having them all dumped into the pound upon reopening. Thousands of pets were pounded during that year, and many of them are still in pound_release and breik_u5.

    The intention was for pound_release pets to be slowly released into the pound, and in fact it worked pretty well for a long time. However, on November 22, 2019, TNT made changes to the code that stopped the release of all pets.

  • How can I tell if a pet is in pound_release?
    • The easiest way to find out is to view the pet's petpage. Pets in pound_release and on breik_u5 will have one of several possible errors on their petpages:




    These two errors were seen between December 20, 2021 (the release of pet slots) and March 31, 2022 (when petlookups were fixed).





    These two errors (an HTTP ERROR 500 message on Chrome and a blank white screen on Firefox) were seen starting March 31, 2022 (when petlookups were fixed).

    Unfortunately, it's impossible to tell from the petpage which pets are in pound_release and which are on breik_u5, although Grundos and pets with four or more numbers in their names are more likely to be on breik_u5.

  • How do I find pound_release pets?
    • You can find them the same way you find stuck pets. Please check out these guides as they are absolutely wonderful and way better at explaining things than I am.

    Lot's PR Guide
    Lorrenn's Stuck Pet Guide
    Stuck searching using "tileset" method

  • Are the times (8:45 and 9:45) still the same for pound_release?
    • No. In October 2019, a bunch of us worked together to narrow down the new release time, which was ~4:08 a.m. and ~4:08 p.m. NST. Like many other automated functions on Neopets, the time moves back a tiny bit each day, so by November, pets were releasing closer to 4:10 a.m. and p.m. NST.

    However, because no pets have been released since the code changes on November 22, 2019, I'm not sure if the time will remain the same—assuming they start up again.

  • What order are pets released in?
    • For more information on the pound_release pattern, see Lot's PR Guide. The main thing to remember is that numbers come first, then letters, then underscores.

  • Well, if underscores come last according to Neo, why do they come first on this page?
    • Because I use a word processing program to update this guide, and it considers underscores to be alphabetically first.

  • How do I find out which pets have been released?
    • Check out our list of Recent Releases or the string tracking guide at ~Devonian.

  • Why have some pets been released out of order?
    • pound_release was a mostly-reliable, mostly-automated process, but occasionally pets have been released out of order. For example, Rosette was released in 2018, but the current Ro- string is nowhere near her yet. I've never been able to find an answer to this question. I sometimes refer to these released-out-of-order pets as "orphans.

    In addition, TNT staff members can go in at any time and manually pull a pet out of pound_release. In 2019, staff member Tony P. replied to a question about pound_release with this explanation:

  • Why are there periods/dots in some of the pet names?
    • Some words/phrases/parts of names accidentally trip the Neopets filters. You can remove the period when you search for or copy the pet's name.

  • Aside from pound_release and breik_u5, are there other special accounts used by TNT?
    • There are a few that I know of, including:
    baduser, an account that holds pets that are deleted because they have inappropriate names
    none, a pet that is used when TNT needs to reverse a pet trade
    testflash, an account that holds Lutaris that have "run away

  • Could you please Neomail me if you find X pet, X word, or UCs?
    • Sorry, but I am unable to message people who are looking for specific things. I'll update this page as frequently as possible to make sure you can find what you need.

  • I found a pet in pound_release, but I don't want to tell anyone about it.
    • No problem! You're under no obligation to share it with me or anyone. You can use the pets here to help you track when it might be released.

  • Will pets on pound_release be purged someday?
    • Probably not. In the past, pound_release and breik_u5 pets were completely unaffected by the purge. Your only hope of getting these names was for them to be released into the pound eventually, and they stayed the same color and species that they were upon going into pound_release. However, a purge hasn't taken place in years and the last one was done when Neopets was owned by a different company, so it's possible that the current TNT will do things differently, if they ever do one.

    For more information on the purge, visit The Purge FAQ.

  • How can I help you?
    • Thank you so much for wanting to contribute! I always welcome messages with names of pets that have been released or new pets that aren't already on the list. It is helpful (although not necessary) if you capitalize it correctly and include the species and color.

  • You haven't answered my question!
    • I'm sorry! Feel free to Neomail me!
